SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-07-26 09:06:21') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-07-26 09:06:21') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-07-26 09:06:21') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-07-26 09:06:25') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-07-26 09:07:08') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-07-26 09:07:08') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-07-26 09:07:09') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-07-26 09:07:09') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-07-26 09:07:12') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-07-26 09:07:12') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id

                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-07-26 09:38:49') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-07-26 09:38:49') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-07-26 09:58:45') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-07-26 09:58:45') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-07-26 09:59:02') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-07-26 09:59:02') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-07-26 09:59:02') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-07-26 09:59:28') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

					  FROM fs_products  WHERE category_id_wrapper LIKE '%,3,%' AND published = 1 ORDER BY ordering ASC LIMIT 30

SELECT id, promotion_id, product_id, quantity, quantity_user, sold, price, percent, `type`, date_end, date_start 
				FROM fs_promotion_discount_detail 
				WHERE published = 1 AND product_id IN (78,79,80) AND DATE(date_end) >= DATE('2024-07-26 09:59:28') 
				AND ((quantity > 0 AND sold < quantity) OR (quantity = 0)) ORDER BY date_start DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-07-26 09:59:28') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC
